Fiji Honey<//user_name>
<text>I recommend the Loco Moco burger with beef marrow gravy! If you know how bone marrow sauce is made, you know the chef put some effort into it and this gravy is quite similar. It's definitely not your typical burger. It won best burger on the L.A. Times 20'. I don't eat spam bacon so I removed it. We also ordered the honey yellow tail and that was just as good, but in a different  way. It wasn't particularly sweet due to the ginger and miso flavors. The ambiance was perfect and the lighting inside is very warm and inviting. Our server was very knowledgeable and helped us decide on drinks because they have a variety of drinks to choose from. On the down side, the drinks are mostly on the sweet side and the ones that are not sweet are amazingly small, but delicious. My only criticism is that some drinks are $14 and you get less than 4 ounces of liquid. Yes, I know! That's a lot for a drink that small. I recommend the Botanical Thyme if you want something refreshing. Also, due to their limited space, expect to wait up to 1 hour outside with no seats so you feel like you are in Disneyland waiting in line. Guests with reservations also have to wait to be seated - not as long though, about 10 minutes.< /text><gmapID>0x80dcd7d79b5200a7:0x7fd343e6dd924e8</gmapID></record>

<review>Spectacular ambiance, with phenomenally crafted cocktails, leaves a recipe for a grade A Tiki bar and Restaurant!

Always, always, always, a great time when I visit, friends, family, or date, the artistically well crafted scenery of a ship wrecked paradise awaits anyone that wants to bask in it's glory.

Top cocktails, Southeast Spice Trade (if your a bourbon fan), Zombie king (if you want that classic tiki experience, and Tarocolada (for that exotic classic drink you can't make at home!).

Service is great, everyone is super courteous and welcoming. There is a lot of pride that goes into the effort each member of the staff puts into creating an awesome experience.<//review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPysrzNroSg_FSr4-m9SwAkbIk9R42sE8dwakMD=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures><Response>None< /Response><gmap_id>0x80dcd7d79b5200a7:0x7fd343e6dd924e8< /gmap_id></record>

<time>1619404148631</time><Rate>5<//Rate><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMffVXv_7abmPHp-5hNaaKHTVHZ0KW82U39slVd=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNB7OYYeh3Oa7bsxqd3cc12utD9KbAjIfWevp4i=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pics><Name>Mary P< /Name>< Gmap_id>

I feel the need to make sure this review is in google maps as well. Lol.

Okay let me start with: this review is long overdue. And I actually almost don't want to write it coz I don't want to share this hidden gem. LOL. But this place is just too awesome, they deserve to be recognized. It's not just the atmosphere that we love - tiki theme. The food here is soooo good, it's addicting! I think we've become regulars. Our favorite is the loco moco burger. It's super juicy! And the combination of flavors just go so well together, I can't explain it but from the gravy to the spam to the bun and the egg it's just all on point! Oh and those fries! Just the right amount of kick to it! And even with a huge portion of serving, we inhale the food so fast coz it's just that good! We've tried a couple of their drinks too. I actually can't remember what the ones on the pictures are, but doesn't matter, they're all good. The flavor profiles of their food and drink are all praise worthy to us. That's why we keep on coming back!

Also the people here are the friendliest. They really are so nice, you can tell they want their customer to have a great experience. And they seem to really like their work and it's not that common to find an establishment with staff that are passionate and proud of their work. Oh! Last note, if you see a long line at the restaurant or you're placed on a long hold over the phone, and you get impatient and get the urge to just cancel your plan, don't! Be patient! It's worth it!< /Text>

Strong Water was fun! Wish you could stay longer than 2 hours because between the strength of the drinks and the food you really want to relax awhile. Great service from the bartenders and wait staff. If Ash is there, try for an off menu specialty (hint hint, it's a play on his name). Mussels are a must. Crabby mushrooms, too. Tales of the Black Lagoon is a new fave drink. The Saturn is also a must try. Captain's Daughter is weirdly refreshing. Pictured: mussels, Captain's Daughter, Taro Colada< /text>

< Review>
I was able to make it to the soft opening last night, and I was impressed. Even with a limited menu and a constant flow of customers this tiki bar is definitely ship shape. The crew is friendly and helpful with drink or food choices and will even give you a tour of the ship.

You can even get reservations for the Captains Quarters, a gin bar that is behind a heavy door. Once again they did not hold back with the decor and it helps keep you immersed in the tale of of this vessel.

I highly recommend you check it out if you enjoy tiki bars, theam bars or craft cocktails.</Review>

<Review>We were there on a Thursday evening around 7pm and it was full. Was lucky enough to get 2 seats. Especially as we were from out of town and weren't going to have a chance to come back. We were greeted by a very friendly and energetic women upon entering. She did a great job chatting us up while our seats were being put together. The decor is nautical themed and not strictly tiki but very well done and put together. Really enjoyed the water feature at the back (as pictured). The menu is a nice blend of original tiki style cocktails mixed with classic tiki drinks with their own subtle twists, not to mention if asked they will make off menu drinks if the ingredients are stocked and the recipe is at hand. Both bar staff that night were chipper and having fun, which makes it a even better experience. Currently they did not have a house tiki mug but was told it is in the works. However that being said they do carry glassware with logo and designed by B.Rex. The food was very good as well and came out pretty quickly.  They also have a semi hidden/secret bar in the back which is reservations only as it only holds about 12 people and is a Gin bar. Also very nice decor. Sad they didn't have a Tiki mug and as were from canada it will be hard to get back to get one, but if we are ever back in Anaheim we will for sure be back.< /Review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP8BULM1CpUnuWMXtLu-dHDPhq4N-IG3tNhkn_x=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures>< Response>

<Review>A large, multi-story shopping mall located on both the North and South sides of Ventura Boulevard. There are two national chain stores, Petco and Michael's. In the lower level is a multi-screen movie theater. There are several restaurants throughout the facility.

Parking on the North side of Ventura Boulevard is located behind the stores. There is underground and above ground parking South of the boulevard. Parking is wheelchair accessible and free. The multi-story structure has an elevator. Underground parking puts your car on the same level as the movie theater. A very comfortable garden, with seating is also located in the lower level.

Located on the North side, behind an unamarmed door is Menchie's Yogurt School. The store in front has a delicious selection of their products.</Review><time>1574713396762<//time><Resp>None< /Resp><user_id>111644673136196029337<//user_id><Name>Cary Brown</Name><gmapID>0x80c29836712d394b:0xcbc89923f834d018</gmapID></record>

If I knew what a nightmare dealing with the leasing staff here would be, I definitely would have considered moving somewhere elsewhere. Unfortunately, being military, we were across the country when deciding on a place and had to have a place ready to move in upon arrival.

We reserved the this unit over 2 months before move-in day (unit was "move-in ready" at the time of reserving), which one  would think would be more than enough time for the property management to ensure things were good to go on their end, right? Wrong.

Before I even get into that, there were a lot of issues dealing with the electronic move-in documents to sign. That should have been a red flag for us. I was away from my spouse at the time due to temporary duty in another state, so we were receiving all the docs via email individually for each of us to sign seperately. Except for I was, but she wasn't. After multiple requests that she gets the documents resent to her email, and property staff (clearly annoyed with HER) insisting the problem was on her end, turns out THEY put an extra 'L' on '"...@gmail.com". On top of that had we had to re sign multiple leases and welcome letters because they kept putting the wrong dates on all the documents even after multiple calls with them confirming dates. The final lease was eventually signed on move-in day.

Parking here is a nightmare, but thankfully residents have a reserved spot, with the option to pay for another. Except for on the day of our arrival, the garage for my unit had not been set up yet, and they were unsure if there were any other available spots, so we were instructed to park outside of the property until the garage guy was able to program the fob the NEXT WEEK. Again, they knew we were coming for 2 months before move in day... My wife's paid parking spot isn't even on the same property as us. Her spot is outside the property gate, across the street, into their other property gate, and down the lot a ways. Honestly it wouldn't be so bad to park outside the gated property if it wasn't for all the homeless mosying around the area.

The apartment has a really convenient Valet Trash service, where they give you a specific bin to leave outside your door each night and somebody collects the trash for you, that way you don't have to deal with the homeless people constantly going thought the property dumpsters. Sounds pretty cool, except for I wouldn't know. The leasing staff neglected to have a bin ready for us until literally the day of me writing this. We followed up with them a few times about it, but they don't answer the phone 90% of the time, and don't respond to voicemails 100% of the time. When we eventually did get into contact with them they said needed to order a new one for us. Ok, understandable, kind of. < Text>
I've thought very long and hard about writing this review. Moving is always a turbulent time in peoples lives and infinity more so during the COVID pandemic. There are no perfect situations and things happen that are often out of our control. All that being said the metro gateway advertises its self as luxury living or at the very least high end.
This is most certainly not the case. I would not go as far as to call living at the metro gateway an unpleasant experience. For the sake of fairness I shall list the things I have enjoyed about my stay at the metro.
1. My neighbors have been pleasant and kept to themselves. Most of them are younger working men and women or small families both tend to keep to themselves (a plus in a pandemic), but I can say with certainty have all been genuinely nice people.
2. It's conveniently close to lots of my favorite eateries and grocery stores. It is also close to the mall but in a pandemic I will consider this a null factor.
3. The front office is accommodating to new tenets (emphasis on new). My girlfriend and I make our money in a lot of unusual ways. We are both freelancers and don't have traditional income sources, but they allowed us to use bank statements over a long period of time to prove we could afford to live at the metro. This is a level of flexibility you cant find everywhere and was a pleasant process.
4. A diverse population. This may be problematic in some ways but as a first generation American and a minority it puts me to ease seeing such a wide range of backgrounds in my neighbors (this provides value to me specifically so feel free to ignore this point).
and that's about it to be honest. There are a lot of bell and whistles they'll try to dangle in front of you but they're not available due to COVID or are negligible considering the price of rent.
THINGS I DISLIKED/COULD NOT STAND
1. COCKROACHES, COCKROACHES, COCKROACHES. There was a pest infestation because of the grills not being cleaned after being used by others and surprise surprise cockroaches made their way all over the place. The metro did very little to deal with this and I wouldn't be surprised if it was a common occurrence. I despise bugs especially roaches. My apartment is kept clean so why do i have to deal with pests because a luxury apartment cant be bothered to clean the common spaces?
2. HOMELESS PROBLEMS. Look, other people being without a home during a global pandemic in riverside county, that's not a surprise at all. As someone who comes from humble beginnings I empathize with the homeless but they dig through the communal dumpsters and leave garbage everywhere! It's not an isolated incident either the same homeless guy is there every morning around 6am like CLOCKWORK. Honestly this guy might as well be advertised as coming with the place at this point. Save your bottles and cans for him and maybe he wont make a huge mess of your garbage looking for them lmao.
3. There's not enough parking. Parking spaces are assigned so no problem right? There's literally only two guest parking spots though so what could go wrong? Well people park in your assigned spot all the time that's what could go wrong! Food delivery people, UPS FEDX people, random guests, you name it they will take your spot while you're at work or shopping for groceries. Call the tow truck then? You can but it wont stop it from happening over and over and over again. If you like having to deal with the hassle of towing people so you can go home after a long day of work then no big deal, but i'd rather not deal with it.
4. Stuff only sorta works. Parking keyfab? replaced twice in a 6 month period. Smart home system? Doesn't come with the code to use and they don't have the code so congrats on your useless hindrance?
4.2 Maintenance is nice enough but they don't wear masks during a global pandemic and instead of fixing the aforementioned smart home system after it triggered the intruder alarm. Easy fix right? have maintenance reset it. They tore it out of the wall and called it a day.
TLDR: The rent is too high live elsewhere.</Text>

< Text>
I had an 18 month lease from December 2018-March 2020.

The good:
Fairly new units with modern floorplan & nice appliances.

The bad:
PARKING!!!! - As you can read in EVERY. SINGLE. REVIEW. since Metro Gateway opened, parking is comical. Each unit is assigned 1 spot (regardless of number of residents) and can purchase an additional spot or garage for $50-100 each month IF there are additional spots available. I tried to get a garage and was put on a waiting list for 9 months. There are 5 guest spots per side of the complex for about 200 units. These spots are occupied 100% of the time by residents (same cars in the spots at all times). You will NEVER be able to have friends over and, if they do come over, they will hate you for the stress of trying to figure the situation out and will never come back. The management will try to tell you they have a new flavor of the month parking policy...(new parking policies were "implemented" 3 times in 18 months and none were ever actually enforced). Because all the guest spots are full, people illegally park in fire lanes and handicap spots daily (sometimes overnight and beyond). Note: When I moved in, the agent told me to just park in the train station when you have guests...Don't do it! Unlike Metro Gateway, they actually have consistent on-site patrol who will write tickets and have vehicles towed.

Management - There was an ownership change to Davlyn that took place about 6 months ago. Previous management was awful about customer service but maintained the property grounds REALLY well. They'd regularly scrub and pressure-wash the hallways, pick up trash in the islands, have crews regularly replace seasonal flowers & mulch, and pick weeds in islands. Maintenance dude was AWESOME - very friendly, attentive, fast, and super thorough! The new staff are more pleasant to deal with but the condition of the property has suffered dramatically. Landscaping and common areas aren't nearly as well-kept as they used to be. Water dispenser was removed from the gym, towels no longer provided, and equipment wipes are always empty. Since they took over, they've had 4 new property managers. We'd get an email or letter introducing us to our new property manager and a week or two later they'd be gone. My last month in the community, my rent did not auto-load in the app, so I called the office and they calculated the total for my final months rent, which I paid that day. Then, I received my move-out statement and their calculation turned out to be a few hundred dollars off so they charged me the difference from my deposit despite it being their (Simone's) clerical error. Also, regardless of the condition of your unit upon move-out, they will charge for paint, carpet, and cleaning...don't waste your time (12hrs) and money ($90) on supplies to clean every spec of dust from the back of the deepest cabinet - it won't matter because they'll assess mandatory charges totaling about $300 (more, I'm sure, if you're a slob).

Terrible residents - The property appears to be somewhat upscale but it's all a facade. If you dare open your windows, you'll get a contact high at any hour of the day because people are endlessly smoking weed in this "no smoking" community - reported countless times with no result. No one cleans up after their pets despite several pet waste stations - urine and smeared dog (I hope) poop in elevators, stairs, walkways, etc. The scrawny wannabe gym bros never clean up after themselves and leave dumbbells, mats, and benches everywhere. Loud music and beer bottles constantly fill the courtyard from authorized and unauthorized gatherings alike.

Pets - My small, older dog was attacked by another (restricted-breed) dog that was not on a leash and had to have surgery (total costs came to around $1,700 in all after follow-up visits). The office staff would not assist us or animal control in locating the owner to pursue legal action against them and their vicious dog.</Text>

I moved in to Metro Gateway, June 2019.  I was impressed with the apartment package, i.e. appliances, decor, location.  I did have some concerns about how well the property would be kept up, and responsiveness of the management and leasing agents.  The first six months of my tenancy turned out to be a terrible experience. <Rating>2< /Rating><Review>There are many words that can be used to describe this apartment complex but the one that is most applicable is ‚Äúsurprising.‚Äù

The apartment itself is quite nice‚Äî it was built within the past 5 years and the amenities are very modern and accessible to all residents. It is a gated community that is split into two sides: the side with the main office and the side with all residents. The insides of the apartments are practically brand new and decorated with modern appliances. The ease of accessibility to nearby train stations, public transport, and abundance of stores made these apartments extremely appealing. However, there are many things about this complex that completely invalidate these perks.

To start, the parking situation. As seen by other reviews of this complex, the parking is, for lack of a better word, shit. Each resident is assigned one spot and one spot only. For residents‚Äô guests, there are at most 5 guest spots on each side of the complex. What happens when all guest spots are taken up? Their solution is to have your guests park at the train station right next door; however, parking at the station is technically prohibited and has resulted in warnings and tickets. Attempting to buy another parking spot or even a garage slot is a long and harboring process and seems like the management team wants to work at least as possible in trying to help their residents. They say that their team routinely walks around the complex to check for violations and concerns, but that is not true as there are cars constantly parked in wrong spots or even illegally on red zones.

Another problem: pets. The amount of pet feces in the planters and even on the asphalt is appalling. There have also been accounts of dogs attacking other dogs (pit bulls specifically, which are prohibited in this complex). Again, if there was a team that routinely checks the complexes, then someone should have noticed at some point that there are prohibited dog breeds within their complex. Not to be unfair to the residents who are responsible pet owners, but the ones who let their dogs run around without leashes should not be allowed to reside at this complex.

All in all, I would not recommend this complex to anyone who is trying to move to the Corona/Riverside area. It is a two star review only because the amenities are actually quite nice and the apartments themselves are clean and practically brand new. However, the cons far outweigh the pros with this place. Along with the problems I listed about, the management staff is also extremely hard to reach, harboring multiple emails and calls before receiving a response. It also seems like if you do not live on the side with the front office, the chances of getting their attention are quite low. If it were not for these issues, this would be a place that I would highly recommend. I hope they can address these issues before it affects any more of their current and future residents.</Review>< pics>

The center's anchor store is the Stater Brothers. There is a bank, some fast food, a bakery and an ice cream store and auto repair shop. The center is located on Palm, the city's main business corridor.
